          <section 
              class=""
              style="background:#ffffff;">
              <p class="toggle-header "
                 style="font-family: 'Open Sans'; font-size: 16px; color:rgb(68, 68, 68);">T</p>
              <div class="toggle-widget-content-wrapper">
                <div class="toggle-widget-content text-widget-content "
                     style="background:#f9f9f9;">
                  <div class="col20 f-left">
                    <p style="line-height: 1.6;"><span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102);">Tachycardia (rapid heart beat. For lab animals only. See also Heart tonic,
</span></p><p style="line-height: 1.6;"><span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102);">Relaxation sets.) - 1.2
</span></p><p style="line-height: 1.6;"><span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102);">Taenia (see Parasites tapeworm)
</span></p><p style="line-height: 1.6;"><span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102);">Taste, none - 10000, 20
</span></p><p style="line-height: 1.6;"><span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102);">Tendomyopathy - 320, 250, 160, 80, 40, 20, 10, 5.8, 2.5, 1.5, 1.2, 1, 0.5
</span></p><p style="line-height: 1.6;"><span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102);">Tetanus (infectious disease of the central nervous system caused by clostridium
</span></p><p style="line-height: 1.6;"><span style="color: rgb(102, 102, 102);">tetani) - 244, 600, 554, 120, 352, 1142, 363, 458, 465, 628
